basaṃta bahāra ke pada (pauṣavadi amāvasyā se mahāsudi 4 taka)

1 (cha? rāga bilāvala #.) vasaṃta paṃcamī ke dina maṃgalā meṃ bilāvala |||
cotāla || āja kī bānika para ho lāla hoṃ bali bali gaī bigalita kaca
subana pāga ḍharaki rahi vāma bhāga aṃga aṃga alasahī || 1|| arūna naiṃna jhapaka
jāta kachu ja~bhāta vāra vāra pīka kapola chahī || dhani suhāga bhāga jākoṃ
'sūra' ke prabhu sa~ga saba nisa bitaī ||2||

2 9 rāga mālakauṃsa eḍa) lahekana lāgī basaṃtabahāra sarik tyoṃ tyoṃ
banavārī lāgyo bahekana || phūle palāsa nakhanāhāra kese teseṃ kānana lāgyo
mahekana ||1|| kokila mora śuka sāra sahaṃsa khaṃjana mīna bhramara akhiyā~
dekha ati lalakana || naṃdadāsa prabhu pyārī agavānī giridhara piyakoṃ dekhata
bhayo śramakana ||2||

(hai rāga mālakoṃsa (ṣcha) cala bana dekha sayānī yamunā taṭa ṭhāḍo chela
gumānī || phūle kadaṃba nāhara palāsa druma trividha pavana sukhasānī ||1|| baharaṃga
kusuma parāga bahaka raho ali lapaṭe guṃjata mṛdabānī || kīra kapota kokilā
dhvani suna ṛtu vasaṃta lahekānī |||2|| suna sakhī vacana mila uṭhī piya soṃ
navanikuṃja kī rānī || bīnana cale doū kusuma kaliyana braja kuṃjana ṛtumānī
|| 3|||

4 (au! rāga mālakoṃsa (ḍara) lahekana lāgīrī basaṃta bahāra māno banavārī
lāgyo bar̤hakana || nā jāno jaba kahā kareṃge lāge hai palāsa drama ḍahakana
||1||| madanabhara kekīḍūka kāḍhata basṇavaraṇa dvuma puṣpalāge mahekana ||| ānaṃda
ghana tuma kita ho birama rahe ita kokilā lāge kuhukana ||2||

5 (7 rāga mālakauṃsa īthḍa) phūlyorī saghana banatā meṃ kokilā karata
gāna ||| calarī bega vṛṣabhāna naṃdinī chār̤a kaṭhina manamāna ||| 1|| nava ṛturāja
āyo nere mila kīje madhupāna || sūradāsa madanamohana priyako māiye rijhāiye
khunāiye mīṭhī madhurī tāna ||2||

śrī dāmodaradāsajī kī badhāī (poḍhavāne)

1 (cha rāga sāraṃga (thjha) āja bacāyo maṃgala cāra || māghamāsa śukla
cotha hai hasta nakṣatra ravivāra ||1|| premasudhā sāgara rasa pragaṭayī ānaṃda

2 chuka rāga sāraṃga ḍara) pragaṭe bhakta śiromaṇī rāya || māghamāsa śukla
cotha adhika loka nidhi āī ||1|| devī jīvake bhāgya udaya bhaye jina
yaha darśana pāī || kari karuṇā prabhu bhūtala āye puṣṭipatha pragaṭāī ||2|| mahā
mahotsava hota pura ghara ghara phūle aṃga na samāī || rasikadāsa cita ehī
cahata he caranakamala mana lāī ||3||

śrīgusāījī tathā śrījayadevajī kī aṣṭapadī

1 cha rāga basaṃta (7) haririha brajayuvatī śatasaṃge | vilasati kariṇī
gaṇa bṛta vāraṇa vara iva rati pati māna bhage ||śru0|| viśrama saṃbhrama lola
vilocana sūcita saṃcita bhāva || kāpi dṛgaṃcala kubalaya nikare raṃcatitaṃ
kalarāvaṃ ||1|| smita ruci ruci ratarānana kamala mudīkṣya hare ratikaṃdaṃ ||
cuṃbati kāpi nitaṃbavatatī karatala dhata cibukamamaṃda || 2|| udabhaṭa bhāvavibhāvita
cāpala mohana nidhuvana śālī ramayatti kāmapipīna ghanastana vilulita nava
vanamālī ||3|| nija pariraṃbha kṛtenudgatarama bhivīkṣya hareṃ savilāsaṃ ||
kāmapikāpi balāda karodgrekutu keṃne sahāsa || 4|| kāmapinīvī baṃca vimokasa
saṃbhrama lajnita nayanāṃ || ramayati saṃprati sumurbari balādapi karatala dhṛta nija
basanāṃ ||5|| piya pariraṃbha vipula pulakāvali dviguṇita subhaga śarīrā ||
uṃdgāyati sakhi kāpi sama̭ hariṇā rati raṇadhīrā ||6|| viśrama saṃbhrama galadaṃ
calamalayāṃcita maṃgamudāra || paśyati sasmita mati vismita manasā sudṛśaḥ
savikāraṃ ||7|| calati kayāpi samaṃsa kara graha mala sata raṃsa bilāsaṃ ||
rādhe taba pūraya tu manoratha mudita midaṃ harirāsaṃ ||8||

2 (cha rāga basaṃta (8) lalita lavaṃga latā pariśīlana komala malaya
samīre || madhukaranikara karaṃbita kokila kūjita kuṃja kuṭīre ||1|| viharatati
haririha sarasavasaṃte || nṛtyati yuvati jane na sama̭ sakhi virahi janasya duraṃte
||dhru0|| un‍mada madana manoratha pathika vadhūjanajanita bilāpe || alikula saṃkula
kusuma samūha nirākula bakula kalāpe || 2|| mṛgamada saurabharabhasa vaśaṃ vadanavadala

rāga bihāga

1 (ha rāga bihāga (up) lāla karata manuhāra rī pyārī māna manāyo ttero ||
madana mohana piya nava nikuṃja meṃ nāma raṭata haiṃ tero |||1|| navala nāgara guna
ke āgara dekha ṛturāja ātho nero || rasika prītama soṃ hilamila bhāminī

2 (| rāga bihāga +śya) pyārī tero mānagaḍha kauna utāre || dina prati
notana hota sakhīrī kauna kāja bicāre ||1|| tere mana kachu ora sakhīrī
mere mana jo ucāre || kāhū misale raṃgana bharīrī giradhara lāla samāre ||2||
yaha samayo hai divasa cāra ko ko yaha nyāva vicāre || hita hari vaṃśa pulina

9 (hara rāga sāraṃga (k‍jha) gahavara rasa saghana nikuṃja chāyātara ropyo ḍola
tahāṃ nāgarī nāgara doū premasuṃ jhūle || bhūṣaṇa aṃga bane hīrāmaṇi kaṭi taṭa
mānoṃ ghanadāminī chabi rājata nali pīta dūkūle ||1|| bīrī khāta khavābata
pramudita mana gāvata sāraṃga rāga gānasoṃ manahī mana phūle || kesara covā agara
julāla ur̤e aura keli kapūrana ghūle ||2|| mṛdaṃga tāla ḍapha bīnā madhura svara
cahu aura gābata upamā kahṭe doū ko samatūle || yaha sukha dekha kona dhīraja
dhare kahe goviṃda suranara muni mana kī gati bhūle ||3||

horī - rasīyā

1 (cha4 rāga horī kāphī ) vana āyau chailā horī kau || malla kāchu siṃgāra
banyo hai yāke pheṃṭā sīsa marorī ko || 1|| soṃdhe san‍yo uparenā sohata yāke māthe
beṃdā rorī ko || parasotama prabhu kuṃvara lāḍilo yaha rijhavāra kiśorī ko ||2||

2 (eka rāga horī kāphī (5) kānā dhare re mukaṭa khele horī ||| ita sthāma
laī picakārī raṃga bhara utta śyāmā kesara ghorī ||1|| hāthana lāla gulāla
pheṃṭa bhara mārata haiṃ bhara bhara jhorī || caṃda sakhī bhaji bālakṛṣṇa chabi tere
badana kamala para cita corī ||2|||

3 (e! rāga horī kāphī īju) horī āīre mohana para raṃga ḍāro || nainana
aṃjana de mana raṃḍana yāke kāna pakara gulacā māro ||1|| kesara meṃ bora karo
raṃga gāro sahe na rahe yaha tana kāro || baṃsī lehdū chināya syāma kī phira pāṃche
nochāvara vāro || 2||

4 (5 rāga horī kāphī 78) darasana de nikasi aṭāmeṃte || umā, ramā,
īdrāṇī, bhavānī, jāke nikasī hai nakha caṃdra chaṭāmeṃte |||1|| rādhejū nikasa
aṭā bhaī ṭhāḍī māno nikasyo hai caṃda ghaṭāmeṃte | puruṣottama prabhu kī chabi
nirakhata māno mākhana nikasyo maṭhā meṃte || 2||
